## Audio and Music [🔝](#readme)

* [Oto](https://github.com/hajimehoshi/oto) ` 🔥 808 `  - ♪ A low-level library to play sound on multiple platforms ♪ ` 📝 3 months ago `
* [PortAudio](https://github.com/gordonklaus/portaudio) ` 🔥 449 `  - Go bindings for the PortAudio audio I/O library ` 📝 8 months ago `
* [music-theory](https://github.com/go-music-theory/music-theory) ` 🔥 337 `  - Go models of Note, Scale, Chord and Key ` 📝 10 months ago `
* [waveform](https://github.com/mdlayher/waveform) ` 🔥 337 `  - Go package capable of generating waveform images from audio streams. MIT Licensed. ` 📝 a year ago `
* [portmidi](https://github.com/rakyll/portmidi) ` 🔥 254 `  - Go bindings for libportmidi ` 📝 7 months ago `
* [id3v2](https://github.com/bogem/id3v2) ` 🔥 189 `  - ID3 decoding and encoding library for Go 
* [flac](https://github.com/mewkiz/flac) ` 🔥 152 `  - Package flac provides access to FLAC (Free Lossless Audio Codec) streams. ` 📝 4 months ago `
* [malgo](https://github.com/gen2brain/malgo) ` 🔥 145 `  - Mini audio library ` 📝 15 days ago `
* [mix](https://github.com/go-mix/mix) ` 🔥 139 `  - Sequence-based Go-native audio mixer for music apps ` 📝 a year ago `
* [GoAudio](https://github.com/DylanMeeus/GoAudio) ` 🔥 127 `  - Go tools for audio processing & creation ` 📝 2 months ago `
* [gaad](https://github.com/Comcast/gaad) ` 🔥 82 `  - GAAD (Go Advanced Audio Decoder) ` 📝 2 months ago `
* [minimp3](https://github.com/tosone/minimp3) ` 🔥 55 `  - Decode mp3 base on https://github.com/lieff/minimp3 ` 📝 2 months ago `
* [vorbis](https://github.com/mccoyst/vorbis) ` 🔥 28 `  - A 'native' ogg vorbis decoder for Go (uses inline stb_vorbis) ` 📝 2 years ago `
* [gosamplerate](https://github.com/dh1tw/gosamplerate) ` 🔥 10 `  - Go Bindings for libsamplerate ` 📝 10 months ago `
  
## Authentication and OAuth [🔝](#readme)

* [oauth2](https://github.com/golang/oauth2) ` 🔥 3.6k `  - Go OAuth2 ` 📝 8 days ago `
* [goth](https://github.com/markbates/goth) ` 🔥 3.2k `  - Package goth provides a simple, clean, and idiomatic way to write authentication packages for Go web applications. ` 📝 4 months ago `
* [authboss](https://github.com/volatiletech/authboss) ` 🔥 2.7k `  - The boss of http auth. ` 📝 24 days ago `
* [go-jose](https://github.com/square/go-jose) ` 🔥 1.8k `  - An implementation of JOSE standards (JWE, JWS, JWT) in Go ` 📝 7 months ago `
* [loginsrv](https://github.com/tarent/loginsrv) ` 🔥 1.8k `  - JWT login microservice with plugable backends such as OAuth2, Google, Github, htpasswd, osiam, .. ` 📝 3 months ago `
* [go-oauth2-server](https://github.com/RichardKnop/go-oauth2-server) ` 🔥 1.7k `  - A standalone, specification-compliant, OAuth2 server written in Golang. ` 📝 7 months ago `
* [osin](https://github.com/openshift/osin) ` 🔥 1.7k `  - Golang OAuth2 server library ` 📝 4 months ago `
* [gologin](https://github.com/dghubble/gologin) ` 🔥 1.4k `  - Go login handlers for authentication providers (OAuth1, OAuth2) ` 📝 3 months ago `
* [gorbac](https://github.com/mikespook/gorbac) ` 🔥 1.2k `  - goRBAC provides a lightweight role-based access control (RBAC) implementation in Golang. ` 📝 16 days ago `
* [scs](https://github.com/alexedwards/scs) ` 🔥 875 `  - HTTP Session Management for Go ` 📝 a month ago `
* [paseto](https://github.com/o1egl/paseto) ` 🔥 507 `  - Platform-Agnostic Security Tokens implementation in GO (Golang) ` 📝 a year ago `
* [permissions2](https://github.com/xyproto/permissions2) ` 🔥 428 `  - Middleware for keeping track of users, login states and permissions ` 📝 9 months ago `
* [jwt](https://github.com/cristalhq/jwt) ` 🔥 259 `  - Safe, simple and fast JSON Web Tokens for Go ` 📝 a month ago `
* [go-guardian](https://github.com/shaj13/go-guardian) ` 🔥 252 `  - Go-Guardian is a golang library that provides a simple, clean, and idiomatic way to create powerful modern API and web authentication. ` 📝 a month ago `
* [jwt](https://github.com/pascaldekloe/jwt) ` 🔥 249 `  - JSON Web Token library ` 📝 3 months ago `
* [jeff](https://github.com/abraithwaite/jeff) ` 🔥 225 `  - Jeff provides the simplest way to manage web sessions in Go. ` 📝 9 months ago `
* [jwt-auth](https://github.com/adam-hanna/jwt-auth) ` 🔥 203 `  - This package provides json web token (jwt) middleware for goLang http servers ` 📝 7 months ago `
* [httpauth](https://github.com/goji/httpauth) ` 🔥 202 `  - HTTP Authentication middlewares ` 📝 5 years ago `
* [branca](https://github.com/hako/branca) ` 🔥 151 `  - Secure alternative to JWT. Authenticated Encrypted API Tokens for Go. ` 📝 9 months ago `
* [sessionup](https://github.com/swithek/sessionup) ` 🔥 111 `  - Straightforward HTTP session management ` 📝 6 months ago `
* [session](https://github.com/icza/session) ` 🔥 107 `  - Go session management for web servers (including support for Google App Engine - GAE). ` 📝 2 years ago `
* [jwt](https://github.com/robbert229/jwt) ` 🔥 89 `  - This is an implementation of JWT in golang! ` 📝 3 years ago `
* [sjwt](https://github.com/brianvoe/sjwt) ` 🔥 87 `  - Simple JWT Golang ` 📝 2 years ago `
* [rbac](https://github.com/zpatrick/rbac) ` 🔥 78 `  - Minimalistic RBAC package for Go applications ` 📝 3 years ago `
* [sessions](https://github.com/adam-hanna/sessions) ` 🔥 59 `  - A dead simple, highly performant, highly customizable sessions middleware for go http servers. ` 📝 a year ago `
* [securecookie](https://github.com/chmike/securecookie) ` 🔥 47 `  - Fast, secure and efficient secure cookie encoder/decoder ` 📝 25 days ago `
* [otpgo](https://github.com/jltorresm/otpgo) ` 🔥 18 `  - Time-Based One-Time Password (TOTP) and HMAC-Based One-Time Password (HOTP) library for Go. ` 📝 3 months ago `
* [go-email-normalizer](https://github.com/dimuska139/go-email-normalizer) ` 🔥 17 `  - Golang library for providing a canonical representation of email address. ` 📝 5 months ago `
* [scope](https://github.com/SonicRoshan/scope) ` 🔥 12 `  - Easily Manage OAuth2 Scopes In Go ` 📝 a year ago `
* [sessiongate-go](https://github.com/f0rmiga/sessiongate-go) ` 🔥 9 `  - A driver for the SessionGate Redis module - easy session management using the Go language. ` 📝 3 years ago `
* [cookiestxt](https://github.com/mengzhuo/cookiestxt) ` 🔥 6 `  - cookiestxt implement parser of cookies txt format ` 📝 2 months ago `
* [casbin](https://github.com/hsluoyz/casbin) ` 🔥 1 `  - An authorization library that supports access control models like ACL, RBAC, ABAC in Golang ` 📝 a month ago `

GO CLI 控制台颜色渲染工具库，支持16色，256色，RGB色彩渲染输出，使用类似于 Print/Sprintf，兼容并支持 Windows 环境的色彩渲染 ` 📝 a month ago `
* [uitable](https://github.com/gosuri/uitable) ` 🔥 611 `  - A go library to improve readability in terminal apps using tabular data ` 📝 2 years ago `

* [tabby](https://github.com/cheynewallace/tabby) ` 🔥 288 `  - A tiny library for super simple Golang tables ` 📝 5 months ago `

* [cfmt](https://github.com/mingrammer/cfmt) ` 🔥 78 `  - Contextual fmt inspired by bootstrap color classes ` 📝 2 years ago `

Argon2 was the winner of the most recent Password Hashing Competition. This is designed for use anywhere password hashing and verification might be needed and is intended to replace imp… ` 📝 5 months ago `

## Middlewares [🔝](#readme)

  
* #### Actual middlewares [🔝](#readme)

    * [Tollbooth](https://github.com/didip/tollbooth) ` 🔥 1.9k `  - Simple middleware to rate-limit HTTP requests. ` 📝 5 months ago`
    * [CORS](https://github.com/rs/cors) ` 🔥 1.8k `  - Go net/http configurable handler to handle CORS requests ` 📝 5 months ago`
    * [Limiter](https://github.com/ulule/limiter) ` 🔥 1.3k `  - Dead simple rate limit middleware for Go. ` 📝 a month ago`
    * [go-server-timing](https://github.com/mitchellh/go-server-timing) ` 🔥 813 `  - Go (golang) library for creating and consuming HTTP Server-Timing headers ` 📝 6 months ago`
    * [go-fault](https://github.com/github/go-fault) ` 🔥 393 `  - Fault injection library in Go using standard http middleware ` 📝 3 months ago`
    * [ln-paywall](https://github.com/philippgille/ln-paywall) ` 🔥 110 `  - Go middleware for monetizing your API on a per-request basis with Bitcoin and Lightning ` 📝 3 years ago`
    * [XFF](https://github.com/sebest/xff) ` 🔥 80 `  - A Golang Middleware to handle X-Forwarded-For Header 
    * [formjson](https://github.com/rs/formjson) ` 🔥 36 `  - Go net/http handler to transparently manage posted JSON 
    * [client-timing](https://github.com/posener/client-timing) ` 🔥 19 `  - An HTTP client for go-server-timing middleware. Enables automatic timing propagation through HTTP calls between servers. ` 📝 3 years ago`
  
* #### Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares [🔝](#readme)

    * [negroni](https://github.com/urfave/negroni) ` 🔥 7k `  - Idiomatic HTTP Middleware for Golang ` 📝 6 months ago`
    * [alice](https://github.com/justinas/alice) ` 🔥 2.3k `  - Painless middleware chaining for Go ` 📝 7 months ago`
    * [render](https://github.com/unrolled/render) ` 🔥 1.4k `  - Go package for easily rendering JSON, XML, binary data, and HTML templates responses. ` 📝 8 days ago`
    * [stats](https://github.com/thoas/stats) ` 🔥 579 `  - A Go middleware that stores various information about your web application (response time, status code count, etc.) ` 📝 2 years ago`
    * [interpose](https://github.com/carbocation/interpose) ` 🔥 292 `  - Minimalist net/http middleware for golang 
    * [renderer](https://github.com/thedevsaddam/renderer) ` 🔥 221 `  - Simple, lightweight and faster response (JSON, JSONP, XML, YAML, HTML, File) rendering package for Go ` 📝 2 years ago`
    * [muxchain](https://github.com/stephens2424/muxchain) ` 🔥 209 `  - Lightweight Middleware for net/http 
    * [rye](https://github.com/InVisionApp/rye) ` 🔥 96 `  - A tiny http middleware for Golang with added handlers for common needs. ` 📝 3 years ago`
    * [gores](https://github.com/alioygur/gores) ` 🔥 94 `  - Go package that handles HTML, JSON, XML and etc. responses ` 📝 5 months ago`
    * [mediary](https://github.com/HereMobilityDevelopers/mediary) ` 🔥 71 `  - Add interceptors to GO http.Client ` 📝 a year ago`
    * [chain](https://github.com/codemodus/chain) ` 🔥 63 `  - Composable chains of nested http.Handler instances. 
    * [go-wrap](https://github.com/go-on/wrap) ` 🔥 59 `  - Go http.Hander based middleware stack with context sharing ` 📝 3 years ago`
    * [catena](https://github.com/codemodus/catena) ` 🔥 7 `  - gRPC interceptor catenation. ` 📝 3 years ago`

Blob store has O(1) disk seek, local tiering, cloud tiering.
